### [235] [OT-UVGS: Revisiting UV Mapping for Gaussian Splatting as a Capacity Allocation Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19127)
*Byunghyun Kim*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: OT-UVGS提出了一种基于最优传输的UV映射方法，通过全局耦合分配来优化UVGS的容量利用率，相比确定性球面投影能显著提升性能指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有UVGS使用确定性球面投影将高斯分布映射到UV位置，这种方法忽略了高斯分布的全局特性，导致许多UV槽位空置而密集区域频繁碰撞，限制了UVGS的潜在容量。

Method: 将UV映射重新解释为固定UV预算下的容量分配问题，提出OT-UVGS：一种轻量级、可分离的一维最优传输启发式映射方法。该方法通过秩排序实现，复杂度为O(N log N)，能够全局耦合分配同时保留原始UVGS表示。

Result: 在184个以对象为中心的场景和Mip-NeRF数据集上，OT-UVGS在相同UV分辨率和每槽容量(K=1)下，一致提升了PSNR、SSIM和LPIPS指标。同时显著改善了UV利用率，包括更高的非空槽位比例、更少的碰撞和更高的高斯保留率。

Conclusion: 仅通过重新设计映射方法就能释放UVGS的显著潜在容量，OT-UVGS可作为球面UVGS的直接替代方案，在保持相同表示结构的同时实现性能提升。

Abstract: UV-parameterized Gaussian Splatting (UVGS) maps an unstructured set of 3D Gaussians to a regular UV tensor, enabling compact storage and explicit control of representation capacity. Existing UVGS, however, uses a deterministic spherical pro- jection to assign Gaussians to UV locations. Because this mapping ignores the global Gaussian distribution, it often leaves many UV slots empty while causing frequent collisions in dense regions. We reinterpret UV mapping as a capacity-allocation problem under a fixed UV budget and propose OT-UVGS, a lightweight, separable one-dimensional optimal-transport-inspired mapping that globally couples assignments while preserving the original UVGS representation. The method is implemented with rank-based sorting, has O(N log N) complexity for N Gaussians, and can be used as a drop-in replacement for spherical UVGS. Across 184 object-centric scenes and the Mip-NeRF dataset, OT-UVGS consistently improves peak signal-to-noise ratio (PSNR), structural similarity (SSIM), and Learned Perceptual Image Patch Similarity (LPIPS) under the same UV resolution and per-slot capacity (K=1). These gains are accompanied by substantially better UV utilization, including higher non-empty slot ratios, fewer collisions, and higher Gaussian retention. Our results show that revisiting the mapping alone can unlock a significant fraction of the latent capacity of UVGS.

</details>


### [236] [Empowering NPC Dialogue with Environmental Context Using LLMs and Panoramic Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19192)
*Grega Radež,Ciril Bohak*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 结合大语言模型与计算机视觉，为游戏NPC提供环境感知能力，使其能动态引用周围物体，提升沉浸感


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统NPC依赖预设对话，缺乏空间理解能力，对玩家行为响应有限，降低了游戏沉浸感

Method: 通过全景图像捕捉NPC环境，应用语义分割识别物体及空间位置，生成结构化JSON表示（包含物体位置和场景图数据），输入LLM使NPC具备空间知识

Result: 用户研究显示参与者更偏好具有环境感知能力的NPC，证实了该方法的有效性

Conclusion: 结合LLM与计算机视觉的方法能有效增强NPC的环境感知能力，提升游戏交互的真实性和沉浸感

Abstract: We present an approach for enhancing non-playable characters (NPCs) in games by combining large language models (LLMs) with computer vision to provide contextual awareness of their surroundings. Conventional NPCs typically rely on pre-scripted dialogue and lack spatial understanding, which limits their responsiveness to player actions and reduces overall immersion. Our method addresses these limitations by capturing panoramic images of an NPC's environment and applying semantic segmentation to identify objects and their spatial positions. The extracted information is used to generate a structured JSON representation of the environment, combining object locations derived from segmentation with additional scene graph data within the NPC's bounding sphere, encoded as directional vectors. This representation is provided as input to the LLM, enabling NPCs to incorporate spatial knowledge into player interactions. As a result, NPCs can dynamically reference nearby objects, landmarks, and environmental features, leading to more believable and engaging gameplay. We describe the technical implementation of the system and evaluate it in two stages. First, an expert interview was conducted to gather feedback and identify areas for improvement. After integrating these refinements, a user study was performed, showing that participants preferred the context-aware NPCs over a non-context-aware baseline, confirming the effectiveness of the proposed approach.

</details>


### [237] [sumo3Dviz: A three dimensional traffic visualisation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19194)
*Kevin Riehl,Julius Schlapbach,Anastasios Kouvelas,Michail A. Makridis*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: SUMO3Dviz是一个轻量级开源3D可视化工具，可将SUMO交通仿真输出转换为高质量3D渲染，支持批量视频生成和第一人称视角，适用于用户研究和教育演示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SUMO交通仿真软件虽然能生成丰富的时空数据，但数值输出和2D可视化在需要直观解释、有效沟通或人本评估的应用中不足，特别是在移动心理学、接受度研究和虚拟体验陈述偏好实验等用户研究中，需要从人类视角感知的真实可视化。

Method: 开发了一个基于Python的轻量级开源3D可视化管道sumo3Dviz，将标准SUMO仿真输出（车辆轨迹和信号状态）转换为高质量3D渲染。该工具独立于专有软件，支持外部摄像头视图和第一人称视角，并优化了批量视频生成。关键技术挑战是轨迹插值和方向平滑，使离散仿真输出产生视觉连贯的运动。

Result: sumo3Dviz是一个可通过pip包管理器安装、跨操作系统运行的开源工具，支持大规模场景可视化、教育演示和自动化实验管道。它解决了从离散仿真数据生成视觉连贯3D动画的技术挑战。

Conclusion: sumo3Dviz提供了一个简单、可脚本化、可复现的解决方案，填补了SUMO交通仿真与高质量3D可视化之间的空白，特别适用于需要人类视角感知的研究和应用场景。

Abstract: Traffic microsimulation software such as SUMO generate rich spatio-temporal data describing individual vehicle movements, interactions, and support the development of control strategies. While numerical outputs and 2D visualisations are sufficient for many technical analyses, they are often inadequate for applications that require intuitive interpretation, effective communication, or human-centred evaluation. In particular, user studies in mobility psychology, acceptance research, and virtual experience stated-preference experiments require realistic visualisations that reflect how traffic scenarios are perceived from a human perspective. This paper introduces sumo3Dviz, a lightweight, open-source 3D visualisation pipeline for SUMO traffic simulations. It converts standard SUMO simulation outputs, such as vehicle trajectories and signal states, into high-quality 3D renderings using a Python-based framework. In contrast to heavyweight game-engine-based approaches or tightly coupled co-simulation frameworks, sumo3Dviz is designed to be simple, scriptable, and reproducible. The tool is installable through the pip package manager, runs across operating systems, and works independently of any proprietary software or licenses. sumo3Dviz supports both external camera views and first-person perspectives, enabling cinematic overviews as well as driver-level experiences. The rendering process is optimized for batch video generation, making it suitable for large-scale scenario visualisation, educational demonstrations, and automated experiment pipelines. A key technical challenge addressed by the tool is trajectory interpolation and orientation smoothing, enabling visually coherent motion from discrete simulation outputs. Source Code on project's GitHub page: https://github.com/DerKevinRiehl/sumo3dviz/.

</details>


### [238] [SketchFaceGS: Real-Time Sketch-Driven Face Editing and Generation with Gaussian Splatting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19202)
*Bo Li,Jiahao Kang,Yubo Ma,Feng-Lin Liu,Bin Liu,Fang-Lue Zhang,Lin Gao*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: SketchFaceGS：首个基于草图实时生成和编辑逼真3D高斯头部模型的框架，通过Transformer预测UV特征和3D增强模块实现高质量重建，支持实时自由视角编辑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然3D高斯表示在数字头部建模中实现了逼真质量和实时渲染，但直观交互的创建和编辑仍然困难。2D草图作为快速直观的概念设计交互方式，存在稀疏、深度模糊、缺乏高频外观线索等问题，难以在实时约束下从笔画推断密集、几何一致的3D高斯结构。

Method: 提出SketchFaceGS框架，采用前馈式粗到细架构：1）基于Transformer的UV特征预测模块从输入草图重建粗糙但几何一致的UV特征图；2）3D UV特征增强模块用高频逼真细节进行细化，生成高保真3D头部。编辑方面引入UV掩码融合技术和分层特征融合策略，实现精确的实时自由视角修改。

Result: 广泛实验表明，SketchFaceGS在生成保真度和编辑灵活性方面优于现有方法，能够通过单次前向传递从草图生成高质量、可编辑的3D头部模型。

Conclusion: SketchFaceGS成功解决了从2D草图实时生成和编辑3D高斯头部模型的挑战，实现了直观交互的头部建模，在生成质量和编辑能力方面表现出色。

Abstract: 3D Gaussian representations have emerged as a powerful paradigm for digital head modeling, achieving photorealistic quality with real-time rendering. However, intuitive and interactive creation or editing of 3D Gaussian head models remains challenging. Although 2D sketches provide an ideal interaction modality for fast, intuitive conceptual design, they are sparse, depth-ambiguous, and lack high-frequency appearance cues, making it difficult to infer dense, geometrically consistent 3D Gaussian structures from strokes - especially under real-time constraints. To address these challenges, we propose SketchFaceGS, the first sketch-driven framework for real-time generation and editing of photorealistic 3D Gaussian head models from 2D sketches. Our method uses a feed-forward, coarse-to-fine architecture. A Transformer-based UV feature-prediction module first reconstructs a coarse but geometrically consistent UV feature map from the input sketch, and then a 3D UV feature enhancement module refines it with high-frequency, photorealistic detail to produce a high-fidelity 3D head. For editing, we introduce a UV Mask Fusion technique combined with a layer-by-layer feature-fusion strategy, enabling precise, real-time, free-viewpoint modifications. Extensive experiments show that SketchFaceGS outperforms existing methods in both generation fidelity and editing flexibility, producing high-quality, editable 3D heads from sketches in a single forward pass.

</details>


### [239] [Stitching Arrowhead Curves: Extending the Sierpinski Arrowhead Curve to Higher Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19287)
*Eric Zimmermann,Stefan Bruckner*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 提出基于繁殖规则的高维Sierpinski箭头曲线扩展方法，并应用于针织服装设计


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Sierpinski三角形已有自然的高维扩展，但Sierpinski箭头曲线缺乏类似的高维扩展方法，需要填补这一空白

Method: 分析二维Sierpinski箭头曲线特性，基于繁殖规则构建任意维度的扩展方法，开发跨层级可视化技术

Result: 成功构建了高维Sierpinski箭头曲线的扩展框架，并实现了跨层级的可视化比较方法

Conclusion: 将几何模式可视化方法应用于针织服装设计，展示了数学分形在时尚艺术中的实际应用价值

Abstract: The Sierpinski triangle and the Sierpinski arrowhead curve are both defined in dimension 2 and can be used to model the same fractal. While a natural extension of the triangular construction to arbitrary dimensions exists, an analogous extension of the curve representation does not. In this article, we analyze the properties of the two-dimensional Sierpinski arrowhead curve to formulate an extension to arbitrary dimensions based on reproduction rules. Building on this formulation, we demonstrate a way to visualize such curves in a comparative manner across levels. Finally, as geometric patterns have a long history in the arts, and especially in fashion, we exemplify this visualization approach in knitwear, specifically in the yoke of a sweater.

</details>


### [240] [SpUDD: Superpower Contouring of Unsigned Distance Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19568)
*Ningna Wang,Xiana Carrera,Christopher Batty,Oded Stein,Silvia Sellán*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 提出一种从离散无符号距离数据重建任意曲面的新方法，利用超功率轮廓概念，在采样密度极限下收敛到真实曲面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无符号距离函数能表示开放、不可定向或非流形曲面，但现有重建方法依赖符号信息、精确梯度或连续距离函数，无法处理离散无符号数据。

Method: 基于距离样本生成功率图，提出超功率轮廓理论概念，证明其在采样密度极限下收敛到真实曲面，并以此作为初始曲面代理设计多边形网格重建算法。

Result: 该方法在离散无符号距离重建任务上大幅优于其他可行策略，为这一数学丰富问题奠定了基础。

Conclusion: 超功率轮廓为离散无符号距离数据重建提供了理论保证，所提算法能有效近似未知真实几何，开启了该领域未来研究的新方向。

Abstract: Unsigned distance functions offer a powerful and flexible implicit surface representation that, unlike their signed counterparts, allow for surfaces that are open, non-orientable, or non-manifold. We consider the problem of reconstructing arbitrary surfaces from a finite set of samples of unsigned distance data. Existing methods for mesh reconstruction from distance data rely on sign information, accurate gradients, a corresponding continuous distance function, or extensive data-dependent training. However, they fail when applied to input that is both discrete and unsigned. Inspired by this challenge, we study the power diagram generated by the distance samples and propose a novel theoretical concept, the superpower contour, which we prove converges to the true surface in the limit of sampling density. We use this superpower contour as an initial surface proxy and design an algorithm that leverages it to produce a polygonal mesh approximating the unknown true geometry. Our method vastly outperforms other conceivable strategies for the discrete unsigned distance reconstruction task, and sets the stage for future work on this mathematically rich problem.

</details>
